\]
So GT consists of exactly: an \(x^3\) term; an \(x t\) term plus an \(x\) term (both linear in \(x\)); and a \(\sin(v)\) term. No \(x^2\), no \(v\), \(v^3\), \(v|v|\), no \(x\sin(\text{something in }t)\), no rational-in-\(x\) denominators, no exponentials.

\]
with \(A=-2.512699...\), \(B=-2.512699...\cdot 0.0921849...\), \(C=-2.512699...\), \(D=-0.77491968...\).

1) \(c0 x^3 + c1 x^2 + c2 v^3 + c3 x + c4 + c5 v + c6 x\sin(c7 t+c8)\).

Even if we kill most terms, remaining structure is rational in \(x\) and/or \(x\sin(\cdot)\), not polynomial \(x^3 + x t + x\), and no \(\sin(v)\). Not match.

Can kill \(x^5,x^2,v\) terms, leaving \(x^3+x\). Still no \(x t\), no \(\sin(v)\). Not match.

49) Polynomial plus rational \(x/(c7 x^2+1)\) plus \(v^5\).  
No \(\sin(v)\), no \(x t\). Not match.

50) \(c0 x + c1 + c2 v x^3 + c3 x e^{c4 t} + c5 v + c6 v\,Max(0,c7 x^2+1) + c8 x^3\).  
No \(\sin(v)\). Also \(x e^{c4 t}\) cannot become \(x t\) on a continuous domain. Not match.

Conclusion: none of the candidates can simultaneously produce both the required \(\sin(v)\) term and the required linear-in-\(t\) term \(x t\) (with no denominators/exponentials), even allowing parameter choices and reasonable domain restrictions.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT: -beta*sin(v) - omega0**c0*(gamma*t + c1)*x - omega0**c2*x**c3

**GT:** `-2.5126990598325*x**3 - 2.5126990598325*x*(0.0921849151045819*t + 1) - 0.774919680656294*sin(v)`

Expanding: `-2.5126990598325*x**3 - 0.231588*x*t - 2.5126990598325*x - 0.774919680656294*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions:
- `x**3`
- `x*t`
- `x`
- `sin(v)`

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce these exact basis functions.

**Key observations:**
- GT requires `sin(v)` as a function of `v`
- GT requires `x*t` (product of x and t)
- GT requires `x**3` and `x`

Let me analyze candidates systematically:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*v**3 + c3*x + c4 + c5*v + c6*x*sin(c7*t + c8)`

Has `x*sin(c7*t+c8)`. For the `x*t` term, we'd need `sin(c7*t+c8) Ōēł linear in t`, which is impossible exactly. For `sin(v)`, it only has `v` and `v**3`, not `sin(v)`. **NO MATCH.**

**Candidate 2:** Contains `Max(0,x)`, `v**3`, `x*sin(c7*t+c8)`. No `sin(v)`, has `Max` which can't replicate `x**3` for negative x. **NO MATCH.**

**Candidate 3:** `c0*x**3 + c1*x**2 + c2*v**3 + c3*x + c4 + c5*v + c6*v*Abs(v) + c7*x*sin(c8*t + c9)`

No `sin(v)`, and `x*sin(c8*t+c9)` can't produce `x*t`. **NO MATCH.**

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*v + c3*v*x**2 + c4*x*Abs(x) + c5*v**3 + c6*x*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9*x**3`

**Candidate 8:** `c0*x/(c1+x┬▓) + c2*v┬│/(c1+x┬▓) + c3*v/(c1+x┬▓) + c4*x*exp(c5*t)/(c1+x┬▓) + c6*v┬│*x┬▓/(c1+x┬▓) + c7*v*x┬▓/(c1+x┬▓) + c8*x┬│*exp(c5*t)/(c1+x┬▓)`
